  hostnamectl set-hostname 'vm1'

# Remove comments and blank lines from /etc/hosts

# Prepend ourselves to /etc/hosts

  sed -i'' '1i 127.0.0.1\tvm1\tvm1' /etc/hosts
}

  /etc/init.d/hostname start || true
